# <a name="_Toc451531408"><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>1<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:

**<span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:

style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>：</span><span lang=EN-US>V5KF</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;

Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>应用配置中的应用账号。</span>

**<span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>站点编号</span>**<span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>：</span><span lang=EN-US>V5KF</span><span

lang=EN-US>[V5KF<span lang=EN-US

mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>后台查看或向客服获取）。</span>

**<span
lang=EN-US>Demo</span>****<span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:

style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;

**<span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:

mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>。</span>

**<span
lang=EN-US>deviceToken</span>**<span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:

lang=EN-US>ID</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

lang=EN-US>64</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>字节以内的字符串。</span>

**<span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>用户</span><span lang=EN-US>ID(uid)</span>**<span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>：标识</span><span lang=EN-US>APP</span><span

Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>，长度为</span><span lang=EN-US>64</span><span

Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>字节以内的字符串。</span>

**<span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:

mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>：使用</span><span lang=EN-US>V5</span><span

Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>智能客服系统的客服人员。</span>**<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span>**

# <a name="_Toc451531409"><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>2<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>功能说明</span></a>

<span
lang=EN-US>V5</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>智能客服系统客户端可集成到</span><span
lang=EN-US>web</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>、</span><span
lang=EN-US>APP</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>等第三方平台提供客户在线咨询服务，实时接收客户的反馈。支持发送文本、位置、图片以及表情等消息，并可显示图文、打开链接。</span>

<span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>本文档介绍</span><span lang=EN-US>V5</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>智能客服系统客户端</span><span lang=EN-US>SDK</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>的</span><span lang=EN-US>iOS</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>版本的集成和使用。本</span><span lang=EN-US>SDK</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>兼容</span><span lang=EN-US>iOS 7.0</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>以上，并为开发者提供</span><span lang=EN-US>Demo</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>工程，可以参照</span><span lang=EN-US>Demo</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>，使用</span><span lang=EN-US>SDK</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>提供的</span><span lang=EN-US>UI</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>快速集成到你的项目中；对</span><span lang=EN-US>UI</span><span

## <a

<![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US

</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>V5KF</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>客服系统账号</span>

<span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>没有</span><span
lang=EN-US>V5KF</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>账号需要前往</span><span
lang=EN-US>[<span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span lang=EN-US>官网</span></span>](http://www.v5kf.com/)</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>注册账号。</span>

<![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>获得应用账号、站点编号</span>

<span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:

mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>应用账号、站点编号作为</span><span

minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>的应用配置界面获取。</span>

<![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>填写对应平台的推送服务器地址</span>

<span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:

<span

<span

## <a
name="_Toc451531419"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:
Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-style-style3d-lightrigtype:13;
mso-style-style3d-lightrigdirection:2;mso-style-style3d-lightrigrotation-anglatitude:
0;mso-style-style3d-lightrigrotation-anglongitude:0;mso-style-style3d-lightrigrotation-angrevolution:
0;font-weight:normal'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>4.3<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Info.plist</span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc451531419'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>配置</span></span>

<span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>由于</span><span lang=EN-US>iOS 9</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>的新特性默认使用</span><span lang=EN-US>ATS</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>，所有网络请求都需要在安全的连接下（当前</span><span
lang=EN-US>App Store</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>尚未强制使用</span><span
lang=EN-US>iOS 9</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>这一新特性），所以一些不兼容的服务需要进行额外的配置，本</span><span
lang=EN-US>SDK</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>使用到了语音和图片服务的</span><span
lang=EN-US>webservice</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>接口，需在</span><span
lang=EN-US>Info.plist</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>添加下述配置：</span>

## <a
name="_Toc451531420"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:
Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-style-style3d-lightrigtype:13;
mso-style-style3d-lightrigdirection:2;mso-style-style3d-lightrigrotation-anglatitude:
0;mso-style-style3d-lightrigrotation-anglongitude:0;mso-style-style3d-lightrigrotation-angrevolution:
0;font-weight:normal'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>4.4<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>关于离线消息推送</span></a>

<span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>客户离线后消息将通过</span><span lang=EN-US>APNs</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>推送到客户端设备，建议使用第三方推送平台，需要在代码中填写您</span><span
lang=EN-US>iOS</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>设备上获取的</span><span
lang=EN-US>deviceToken</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>，并在</span><span
lang=EN-US>V5</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>后台配置推送平台的信息，否则离线后接收不到消息。</span>

# <a name="_Toc451531421"><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>5<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>使用</span><span
lang=EN-US>SDK</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc451531421'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>提供的</span><span lang=EN-US>UI</span></span><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc451531421'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>快速集成</span></span>

<a
name="_Toc451531422"></a><a name="_Ref440446884"><span style='mso-bookmark:
_Toc451531422'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:
Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-style-style3d-lightrigtype:13;
mso-style-style3d-lightrigdirection:2;mso-style-style3d-lightrigrotation-anglatitude:
0;mso-style-style3d-lightrigrotation-anglongitude:0;mso-style-style3d-lightrigrotation-angrevolution:
0;font-weight:normal'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>5.1<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>初始化</span><span lang=EN-US>SDK</span></span></a>

<span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>将</span><span lang=EN-US> SDK </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>文件添加到工程后，在</span><span lang=EN-US>AppDelegate</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>中</span><span lang=EN-US>import “V5ClientAgent.h&nbsp;“</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>文件，然后在</span><span lang=EN-US>application:
willFinishLaunchingWithOptions:</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>函数中初始化</span><span
lang=EN-US> SDK </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>。示例如下：</span>

<table class=MsoTableGrid border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none;mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;

 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:0;mso-yfti-firstrow:yes;mso-yfti-lastrow:yes;
  height:31.55pt'>
  <td width=568 valign=top style='width:426.1pt;border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;

`<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt'>- (BOOL)application:(UIApplication
  *)application didFinishLaunchingWithOptions:(NSDictionary *)launchOptions {<o:p></o:p></span>`

`<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt'><span

  customization after application launch.<o:p></o:p></span></span>`

`<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span>// </span>``<span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:

  accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>初始化</span>``<span lang=EN-US
  style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:
  191'>SDK<o:p></o:p></span>`

`<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt'><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>[V5ClientAgent
  initWithSiteId:@&quot;10000&quot;<o:p></o:p></span>`

`<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt'><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>account:@&quot;v5kf&quot;<o:p></o:p></span>`

`<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt'><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>exceptionDelegate:nil];<o:p></o:p></span>`

`<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt'><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span>`

`<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt'><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>return YES;<o:p></o:p></span>`

`<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt'>}</span>`

  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>其中</span><span lang=EN-US>siteId</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>和</span><span lang=EN-US>account</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>分别是从</span><span lang=EN-US>V5</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>后台可以获取到的站点编号和应用账号。</span>

## <a
name="_Toc451531423"></a><a name="_Ref440446942"><span style='mso-bookmark:
_Toc451531423'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:
Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-style-style3d-lightrigtype:13;
mso-style-style3d-lightrigdirection:2;mso-style-style3d-lightrigrotation-anglatitude:
0;mso-style-style3d-lightrigrotation-anglongitude:0;mso-style-style3d-lightrigrotation-angrevolution:
0;font-weight:normal'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>5.2<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>用户信息和参数设置</span></span></a>

<span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>使用</span><span lang=EN-US>SDK</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>提供的</span><span lang=EN-US>UI</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>集成，需要在**启动会话界面**之前进行用户信息和参数配置</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:"Courier New";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Courier New";color:black;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>。配置项如下：</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";
color:black;mso-font-kerning:0pt'><o:p></o:p></span>

<table class=MsoTableGrid border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none;mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
 mso-yfti-tbllook:1184;mso-padding-alt:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:0;mso-yfti-firstrow:yes;mso-yfti-lastrow:yes;
  height:162.35pt'>
  <td width=568 valign=top style='width:426.1pt;border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;height:162.35pt'>

`<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'>//</span>``<span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";mso-fareast-font-family:
  宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:"Courier New";
  color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>需要</span>``<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'>#import &quot;V5ClientAgent.h&quot;<o:p></o:p></span>`

`<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'>// </span>``<span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";mso-fareast-font-family:
  宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:"Courier New";
  color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>获得</span>``<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'>V5ClientAgent</span>``<span style='font-size:
  10.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";mso-fareast-font-family:
  宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:"Courier New";
  color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>配置项</span>``<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'><o:p></o:p></span>`

`<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt'>V5Config *config = [V5ClientAgent
  shareClient].config;<o:p></o:p></span>`

`<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'>// </span>``<span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";mso-fareast-font-family:
  宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:"Courier New";
  color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>设置用户信息，坐席端可查看</span>``<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'><o:p></o:p></span>`

`<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt'>config.nickname = @&quot;test</span>``<span
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";
  mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
  "Courier New"'>－张三</span>``<span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt'>&quot;;<o:p></o:p></span>`

`<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt'>config.gender = 1;<span style='color:
  #538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'> //</span></span>``<span
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";
  mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
  "Courier New";color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>性别：</span>``<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'>0-</span>``<span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";mso-fareast-font-family:
  宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:"Courier New";
  color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>未知</span>``<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'> 1</span>``<span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";mso-fareast-font-family:
  宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:"Courier New";
  color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>－男</span>``<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'> 2</span>``<span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";mso-fareast-font-family:
  宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:"Courier New";
  color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>－女</span>``<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'><o:p></o:p></span>`

`<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt'>config.avatar = @&quot;</span>``<span
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";
  mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
  "Courier New"'>头像</span>``<span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt'>URL&quot;;<span
  style='color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'> //</span></span>``<span
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";
  mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
  "Courier New";color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>客户头像</span>``<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'>URL<o:p></o:p></span>`

`<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt'>config.uid =
  @&quot;ios-user-id-for-test&quot;;<span style='color:#538135;mso-themecolor:
  accent6;mso-themeshade:191'> //</span></span>``<span
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";

  "Courier New";color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>用户唯一</span>``<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'>ID,</span>``<span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";mso-fareast-font-family:
  宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:"Courier New";
  color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>不同的</span>``<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'>uid</span>``<span style='font-size:10.0pt;

  color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>消息记录单独保存</span>``<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'><o:p></o:p></span>`

`<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span>`

`<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;

  color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>用户信息单次设置即生效，更新用户信息或者切换用户时需调用</span>``<span

## <a
name="_Toc451531424"></a><a name="_Ref437850816"><span style='mso-bookmark:
_Toc451531424'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:
Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-style-style3d-lightrigtype:13;
mso-style-style3d-lightrigdirection:2;mso-style-style3d-lightrigrotation-anglatitude:
0;mso-style-style3d-lightrigrotation-anglongitude:0;mso-style-style3d-lightrigrotation-angrevolution:
0;font-weight:normal'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>5.3<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>启动会话界面</span></span></a>

<span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>通过简单地添加一个在线咨询按钮即可使用智能客服客户端功能，在按钮点击事件处理中加入启动会话界面的代码：</span>

<table class=MsoTableGrid border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='margin-left:-1.7pt;border-collapse:collapse;border:none;mso-border-alt:
 solid windowtext .5pt;mso-yfti-tbllook:1184;mso-padding-alt:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:0;mso-yfti-firstrow:yes;mso-yfti-lastrow:yes;
  height:51.0pt'>
  <td width=570 valign=top style='width:427.8pt;border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;height:51.0pt'>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";mso-font-kerning:
  0pt'>V5ChatViewController *chatViewController = [V5ClientAgent
  createChatViewController];<o:p></o:p></span>

<span lang=EN-US
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;mso-themecolor:
  accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>// </span><span
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";
  mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
  "Courier New";mso-bidi-font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;mso-themecolor:
  accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>不显示底部栏（有底部栏的需加此配置）</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;
  mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'><o:p></o:p></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";mso-font-kerning:
  0pt'>chatViewController.hidesBottomBarWhenPushed = YES;<o:p></o:p></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";mso-font-kerning:
  0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span>

<span lang=EN-US
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;mso-themecolor:
  accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>/* </span><span
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";
  mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
  "Courier New";mso-bidi-font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;mso-themecolor:
  accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>下面为会话界面配置，非必须，可根据需求自定义配置，均有默认值</span><span
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;mso-themecolor:
  accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'> <span lang=EN-US>*/<o:p></o:p></span></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;
  mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>// </span><span
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";
  mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
  "Courier New";mso-bidi-font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;mso-themecolor:
  accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>会话界面的代理</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;
  mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>V5ChatViewDelegate<o:p></o:p></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;
  mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span lang=EN-US
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>chatViewController.delegate = self;<span
  style='color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'><o:p></o:p></span></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;
  mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span lang=EN-US
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";mso-font-kerning:0pt'>chatViewController.deviceToken
  = @&quot;</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  "Courier New";mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
  mso-hansi-font-family:"Courier New";mso-bidi-font-family:"Courier New";
  mso-font-kerning:0pt'>设备的</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:"Courier New";mso-font-kerning:0pt'>deviceToken&quot;;<span
  style='color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'> //&nbsp;</span></span><span
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";
  mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
  "Courier New";mso-bidi-font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;mso-themecolor:
  accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>也可在</span><span lang=EN-US
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;mso-themecolor:
  accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>config</span><span
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";
  mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
  "Courier New";mso-bidi-font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;mso-themecolor:
  accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>设置</span><span lang=EN-US
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;mso-themecolor:
  accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>deviceToken<o:p></o:p></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;
  mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>// </span><span
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";
  mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
  "Courier New";mso-bidi-font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;mso-themecolor:
  accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>允许并设置消息铃声</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;
  mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>SystemSoundID<o:p></o:p></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;
  mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span lang=EN-US
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";mso-font-kerning:0pt'>chatViewController.allowSound
  = YES;<span style='color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'><o:p></o:p></span></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;
  mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span lang=EN-US
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";mso-font-kerning:0pt'>chatViewController.soundID
  = 1007;<span style='color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'><o:p></o:p></span></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;
  mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>// </span><span
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";
  mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
  "Courier New";mso-bidi-font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;mso-themecolor:
  accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>允许发送语音</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;
  mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'><o:p></o:p></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;
  mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span lang=EN-US
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";mso-font-kerning:0pt'>chatViewController.enableVoiceRecord
  = YES;<span style='color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'><o:p></o:p></span></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#538135;
  mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>// </span><span

<span

<![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

<span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;

"Courier New";mso-bidi-font-family:"Courier New";mso-font-kerning:0pt'>协议中实现</span><span

Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>方法</span><span lang=EN-US

<span

  "Courier New";mso-font-kerning:0pt'>- (V5Message
  *)userWillSendMessage:(V5Message *)message {<o:p></o:p></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:
  "Courier New";mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>if (userViewSomething) { <span
  style='color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>//</span></span><span
  style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  "Courier New";mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
  mso-hansi-font-family:"Courier New";mso-bidi-font-family:"Courier New";
  color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:
  0pt'>用户浏览某商品的标识</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:"Courier New";mso-font-kerning:0pt'><o:p></o:p></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:
  "Courier New";mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span>message.customContent = @{@&quot;</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";
  mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
  "Courier New";mso-bidi-font-family:"Courier New";mso-font-kerning:0pt'>用户等级</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:
  "Courier New";mso-font-kerning:0pt'>&quot;: @&quot;VIP&quot;,<o:p></o:p></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:

<a
name="_Toc451531430"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>开启消息服务</span></a>

<span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>开启消息服务一般在</span><span lang=EN-US>UIViewController</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>页面打开时进行，具体接口参考如下：</span>

<table class=MsoTableGrid border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none;mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;

  accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>//</span>``<span style='font-size:

  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'><o:p></o:p></span>`

  shareClient] startClientWithDelegate:self];<o:p></o:p></span>`

  </td>
 </tr>

<span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>其中</span><span lang=EN-US>UIViewController</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>需实现协议</span>**<span lang=EN-US>V5MessageDelegate</span>**<span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>，初始化内容包括：</span>

<![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>1.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>设置消息回调监听器；</span>

<![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>2.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>向</span><span
lang=EN-US>V5</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>认证服务进行客户端认证，根据初始化时的站点信息和客户端生成的客户</span><span
lang=EN-US>ID</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>向认证服务器认证（这之前可进行客户端用户信息设置，参见</span><!--[if supportFields]><span
lang=EN-US><span style='mso-element:field-begin'></span> REF _Ref440446942 \r
\h <span style='mso-element:field-separator'></span></span><![endif]--><span
lang=EN-US>5.2<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <w:data>08D0C9EA79F9BACE118C8200AA004BA90B02000000080000000E0000005F005200650066003400340030003400340036003900340032000000</w:data>
</xml><![endif]--></span><!--[if supportFields]><span lang=EN-US><span
style='mso-element:field-end'></span></span><![endif]--><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>），获取会话参数；</span>

<![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>3.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>认证成功并返回参数后建立会话连接，消息服务开启完成。</span>

<span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>此外，提供关闭消息服务方法：</span>

  stopClient]; <span style='color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:
  191'>//</span></span>``<span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:

<a
name="_Toc451531431"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:
Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-style-style3d-lightrigtype:13;
mso-style-style3d-lightrigdirection:2;mso-style-style3d-lightrigrotation-anglatitude:
0;mso-style-style3d-lightrigrotation-anglongitude:0;mso-style-style3d-lightrigrotation-angrevolution:
0;font-weight:normal'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>6.4<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>消息代理</span></a>

<span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>消息代理的声明在</span><span lang=EN-US>V5Delegate.h</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>中有说明，会话界面的</span><span lang=EN-US>UIViewController</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>需要实现协议</span><span lang=EN-US>V5MessageDelegate</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>实现消息接收和发送结果的回调等方法，具体说明如下：</span>

<table class=MsoTableGrid border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none;mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
 mso-yfti-tbllook:1184;mso-padding-alt:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:0;mso-yfti-firstrow:yes;mso-yfti-lastrow:yes'>
  <td width=568 valign=top style='width:426.1pt;border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:
  "Courier New";mso-font-kerning:0pt'>@protocol V5MessageDelegate
  &lt;NSObject&gt;<o:p></o:p></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;color:#3F7F5F;
  mso-font-kerning:0pt'>/**<o:p></o:p></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;color:#3F7F5F;
  mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>* </span><span
  style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;
  mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:#3F7F5F;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>收到即时消息</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;color:#3F7F5F;
  mso-font-kerning:0pt'><o:p></o:p></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;color:#3F7F5F;
  mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>* @param
  message </span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;
  font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
  mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:#3F7F5F;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>消息对象，元素为</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;color:#3F7F5F;
  mso-font-kerning:0pt'>V5Message</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
  minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
  color:#3F7F5F;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>类型</span><span lang=EN-US
  style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;color:#3F7F5F;mso-font-kerning:
  0pt'><o:p></o:p></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;color:#3F7F5F;
  mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>*/<o:p></o:p></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:
  "Courier New";mso-font-kerning:0pt'>- (void)receiveV5Message:(V5Message
  *)message;<o:p></o:p></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;color:#3F7F5F;
  mso-font-kerning:0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;color:#3F7F5F;
  mso-font-kerning:0pt'>/**<o:p></o:p></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;color:#3F7F5F;
  mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>* </span><span
  style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;
  mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:#3F7F5F;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>收到即时消息</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;color:#3F7F5F;
  mso-font-kerning:0pt'>--JSON</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
  minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:#3F7F5F;
  mso-font-kerning:0pt'>字符串</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;
  mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;color:#3F7F5F;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>(</span><span
  style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;
  mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:#3F7F5F;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>接口扩展预留</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;color:#3F7F5F;
  mso-font-kerning:0pt'>)<o:p></o:p></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;color:#3F7F5F;
  mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>* @param
  json JSON</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;
  font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
  mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:#3F7F5F;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>字符串消息，元素为</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;color:#3F7F5F;
  mso-font-kerning:0pt'>NSString</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
  minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
  color:#3F7F5F;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>类型</span><span lang=EN-US
  style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;color:#3F7F5F;mso-font-kerning:
  0pt'><o:p></o:p></span>

<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;color:#3F7F5F;
  mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>*/<o:p></o:p></span>

  mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>* @param status
  KV5ClientServingStatus</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:

  mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>中的定义</span><span lang=EN-US

  0pt'><o:p></o:p></span>

  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;color:#3F7F5F;
  mso-font-kerning:0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>*/<o:p></o:p></span>

  "Courier New";mso-font-kerning:0pt'>- (void)servingStatusChange:(KV5ClientServingStatus)status;<o:p></o:p></span>

`<span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:

`<span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:

  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>*<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;
  </span></span>``<span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:宋体;

  accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>获得开场消息</span>``<span lang=EN-US
  style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:
  191'><o:p></o:p></span>`

`<span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:
  accent6;mso-themeshade:191'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>*
  @param mode<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>KV5ClientOpenMode</span>``<span
  style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";
  mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
  "Courier New";color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>详见</span>``<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'>V5Defination</span>``<span style='font-size:
  10.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";mso-fareast-font-family:
  宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:"Courier New";
  color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>中</span>``<span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;
  mso-themeshade:191'>KV5ClientOpenMode<o:p></o:p></span>`

`<span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:
  accent6;mso-themeshade:191'><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>*<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;
  </span>@param patam </span>``<span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Courier New";mso-fareast-font-family:
  宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:"Courier New";
  color:#538135;mso-themecolor:accent6;mso-themeshade:191'>参数根据不同模式设置</span>``<span

  mso-themeshade:191'><o:p></o:p></span>`

`<span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;color:#538135;mso-themecolor:
  accent6;mso-themeshade:191'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>*/<o:p></o:p></span>`

`<span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt'>-
  (void)getOpeningMessageOfMode:(KV5ClientOpenMode)mode <o:p></o:p></span>`

  NSString *)param;</span>`

<![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US

style='mso-list:Ignore'>2.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

<![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>3.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>【增加】</span><span
lang=EN-US>V5Message</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>增加字典类型属性</span><span
lang=EN-US>customContent</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>，支持添加自定义参数到消息，将透明传输到坐席端，比如可在用户提问中加入用户刚刚正查看的商品信息，消息自定义参数仅当次传输有效，服务端不做保存。</span>

<![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>4.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>【修复】修复不同坐席头像只显示当前坐席头像问题。</span><span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span>

<![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
